Department of State Accounts, Ministry of Finance and Planning, Mr. Thosapala Hewage, Secretary, Ministry of Enterprise Development and Investment Promotion, Dr. Rohan Perera, Legal Adviser, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Saliya Wickramasuriya, Chairman, Sri Lanka Ports Authority, Dr. (Mrs.) Rani Jayamaha, Deputy Governor, Central Bank and Dr. Neil R. de Silva, Director-General of the Petroleum Resources Development Secretariat as members. අෙප් බිමල් රත්නායක මන්තීතුමා ඇහුවා, ෙඩොක්ටර් නීල් ද සිල්වා විතරද ෙම් තාක්ෂණය ගැන ෙත්රුමක් තිෙයන ෙකෙනකුට ඉන්ෙන් කියා. ඔහු අපට වැරදි අවෙබෝධයක් ෙදනවා කියලා කිව්වා. එෙහම ෙචෝදනා කරන්න නරකයි. ෙමොකද, එතුමා විතරයි ඉන්ෙන්. ෙවන කවුරුවත් නැහැ. එතුමාට ෙම් විධියට ෙචෝදනා කළාම "මට ෙම් රක්ෂාව ඕනෑ නැහැ." කියලා සමහර ෙවලාවට ෙම්ක දාලා යන්න පුළුවන්. "මම ෙම් පිට රට රක්ෂාවක් දාලා, ලංකාවට ආදෙර් නිසා ෙමෙහේ ආවා. ෙම් ෙතොරතුරු ෙසොයා ෙගන ලංකාවට පෙයෝජනයක් වන විධියට කටයුතු කරනවාය කියලා හිතා ෙගන ආපු මට පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුෙව්දී ෙම් වෙග් ෙචෝදනා කරනවා නම් මට ෙම් රක්ෂාව ඕනෑ නැහැ." කියලා යන්න පුළුවන්. ඊට පස්ෙසේ අපට උඩ බිම බලන්න ෙවයි. ෙම් විධියට ෙත්රුමක් නැති කථා කියන එක වැරදියි. ෙඩොක්ටර් නීල් ද සිල්වා කියන්ෙන්, ෙහොඳ දැනුමක් තිෙබන, ෙහොඳ ෙත්රුමක් තිෙබන පුද්ගලෙයක් බව මා ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී මතක් කර ෙදන්න කැමැතියි.

The TEC was appointed as per the directive of the Cabinet of Ministers to assist the CANC in view of the highly technical nature of the subject. As part of the evaluation process, the TEC and the CANC did a thorough study of the model PRA from which the signed PRA was derived. The TEC assisted the CANC to evaluate the bids submitted for Block No. 1 and the CANC made recommendation to the Cabinet that the best proposal was submitted by Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited with the suggestion that the Petroleum Resource Agreement with Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited should be signed with the concurrence of the Attorney-General’s Department. ෙම් ෙකයාන් සමාගෙමන් තමයි ෙහොඳම ෙයෝජනා; අපට වාසි වන විධිෙය් ෙයෝජනා ඉදිරිපත් කර තිබුෙණ්. අපි එපා කිව්වා නම් ඒ ෙගොල්ලන් යනවා. එතෙකොට ආපහු පරණ තත්ත්වයටයි යන්න සිද්ධ ෙවන්ෙන්. ෙම් ගෙව්ෂණ කටයුතු කරන්නට ආපහු කවුරුවත් එන්ෙන් නැහැ. අපි ෙටන්ඩර් කැ ෙඳව්වත් කවුරුවත් එන්ෙන් නැහැ. එතෙකොට කියයි, "අපි ෙටන්ඩර් දැම්මා. අපිට ෙම්ක දුන්ෙන් නැහැ. ඒක නිසා වැඩක් නැහැ."යි කියලා. ඊට පස්ෙසේ කාටවත් එන්නට වුවමනාවක් නැහැ. ෙමොකද, ෙවනත් රටවල ෙතල් තිෙයනවා. ෙතල් තිෙයන රටවලට තමයි යන්ෙන්. ෙම්ක ෙතල් නැති රටක්. ෙතල් තිෙයනවා කියලා ස්ථිර වශෙයන් අපට කියන්න බැහැ. ෙතල් තිෙයනවා. නමුත් ෙව ළඳාම් කරන්න පුළුවන් තත්ත්වයකට ෙතල් තිෙයනවාද නැද්ද කියලා කවුරුවත් හඳුනා ෙගන නැහැ. ඒකට තව seismic study එකක් කරන්න ඕනෑ. ඉතින් එෙහම විශ්වාසෙයන්, බයක් නැතිව ෙම් සමාගම ආවා නම් අපි ඒ සමාගමත් එක්ක සම්බන්ධ ෙවලා අපට වාසි ලබා ගන්න පුළුවන් කමයක් හදා ෙගන කටයුතු කරනවා මිස අපට වුවමනා නැති ෙද්වල් ඉල්ලන්න ගියා නම් අන්තිමට කවුරුවත් නැති ෙවනවා, ෙම් ෙවළඳාම කරන්න; ෙම් ගෙව්ෂණ කරන්න. The Attorney-General advised that the selected party, namely Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited, should incorporate a subsidiary company and the subsidiary company should enter into a PRA with the Government. Accordingly, a

company named Cairn Lanka (Pvt.) Limited was incorporated in Sri Lanka and this company entered into a PRA with the Government on 7th July, 2008. Thus, you will see that throughout the process, a maximum degree of professionalism and transparency had been adopted. Before signing the Agreement, care has been taken to analyze the PRA well and design it to ensure that the country gets the best deal through the awarded tender while, at the same time, it is attractive to prospective oil and gas exploration companies. If we are unable to attract oil and gas companies for reasons like high competition from countries that have already made discoveries and offer more lenient fiscal terms than ours, there would be no oil revenue for us to talk about. Attracting oil exploration companies to countries like Sri Lanka, where the acreage is in deep water and since there have been no premium discoveries, will be a difficult task because there is much acreage available in other oil producing countries. India just concluded the NELP VI Licensing round and 15 of their blocks did not get any bids. In awarding the tender to Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited, we had to take into consideration the company profile too. Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited has been in South Asia for more than a decade and has developed a good knowledge and understanding of the geology of the region. The company has made over 40 oil and gas discoveries in India, including the famous and world-class Mangala onshore oil discovery in the deserts of Rajastan in North West India. Cairn India (Pvt.) Limited, listed in the Bombay Stock Exchange, is now an autonomous company with a market capitalization of over US Dollars 11 billion. It is among the top 25 companies in India and Cairn Energy PLC of Scotland is a major shareholder of the company. It operates two processing plants, 11 offshore platforms and 200 kilometres of sub-sea pipelines. It has exploration interests in 14 blocks across India with a net operated production of approximately 75,000 barrels of oil and gas. We are lucky to have entered into this Agreement from which we stand to gain many benefits. I am happy to state some of the major benefits. We have already received one million US Dollars as signature bonus at the time of signing the Agreement. US Dollars 50 million as production bonus is to be paid at the time of commencement of commercial production. There will be a 10 per cent royalty on every barrel of oil and every cubic metre of gas produced. Tax will be on contractor’s profit according to the income tax law of our country. There will be a 15 per cent participation by the National Oil Company. We will have a National Oil Company and that will have 15 per cent participation. Also there will be a profit share to the Government that increases with time. Then, the next is the use of Sri Lankan goods and services. The country would benefit very much from their spending schedule which is

2008 සැප්තැම්බර් 10 423 424

expected to be around US Dollars 112 million. There will be employment opportunities and education and training in Petroleum Science for Sri Lankans. Technology transfer to Sri Lanka and funds to conduct environmental research are also expected. The company is bound to commence work in the next six months that follows the signing of the PRA. After all, it is a risky investment the company is making. It is akin to gambling. Nobody can say whether you will find a commercial quantum of hydrocarbon deposit. In India, bids were called for 152 blocks and there were discoveries only in 15 blocks, indicating a failure rate of 90 per cent. So, the larger the area of exploration, the better the chances of finding oil. Therefore, please do understand the amount of benefit we stand to gain by any chance of commercial discovery of oil in our first attempt itself. Be optimistic and join the whole country in one prayer and wish the best for the country.

I am proud that I have been privileged to activate the much talked about and much delayed oil exploration in Sri Lanka as part of the "Mahinda Chintana" to carry forward the country to economic prosperity. I am thankful to President Mahinda Rajapaksa for all the encouragement given to go ahead to achieve our determined goal. Thank you. පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව අ. භා. 3.00ට, 2008 සැප්තැම්බර් 11 වන බහස්පතින්දා පූ.භා. 9.30 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය.

அதன்பᾊ பி. ப. 3.00 மணிக்கு பாராᾦமன்றம், 2008 ெசப்ெரம்பர் 11, வியாழக்கிழைம ᾙ.ப. 9.30 மணிவைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ. Adjourned accordingly at 3.00 p.m. until 9.30 a.m. on Thursday, 11th September, 2008.

குறிப்ᾗ

உᾠப்பினர் இᾠதிப் பதிப்பிற் ெசய்யவிᾞம்ᾗம் பிைழ திᾞத்தங்கைளத் தமᾐ பிரதியில் ெதளிவாகக் குறித்ᾐ அதைனப் பிைழ

திᾞத்தப்படாத பிரதி கிைடத்த இᾞ வாரங்கᾦள் ஹன்சாட் பதிப்பாசிாியᾞக்கு அᾔப்ᾗதல் ேவண்ᾌம்.

සැ.යු. ෙමම වාර්තාෙව් අවසාන මුදණය සදහා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුතු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්තීන් මින් පිටපතක් ෙගන නිවැරදි කළ යුතු ආකාරය එහි පැහැදිලිව ලකුණු ෙකොට, පිටපත ලැබී ෙදසතියක් ෙනොඉක්මවා හැන්සාඩ් සංස්කාරක ෙවත ලැෙබන ෙසේ එවිය යුතුය.

சந்தா ; ஹன்சாட் அதிகார அறிக்ைகயின் வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾟபா 2,178. ஹன்சாட் தனிப்பிரதி ᾟபா 18.15. தபாற் ெசலᾫ ᾟபா 2.50. வᾞடாந்த சந்தா ᾙற்பணமாக அத்தியட்சகர், அரசாங்க ெவளியீட்டᾤவலகம், இல. 132, மாயா அெவனிᾜ, கிᾞளப்பைன, ெகாᾨம்ᾗ 5 என்ற விலாசத்திற்கு அᾔப்பி பிரதிகைளப் ெபற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளலாம். ஒவ்ேவாராண்ᾌம் நவம்பர் 30 ஆந் ேததிக்கு ᾙன் சந்தாப் பணம் அᾔப்பப்பட ேவண்ᾌம். பிந்திக் கிைடக்கும் சந்தா விண்ணப்பங்கள் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்படமாட்டா.

දායක මුදල්: පාර්ලිෙම්න්තු විවාද වාර්තාවල වාර්ෂික දායක මිල රු.2178කි. පිටපතක් ෙගන්වා ගැනීම අවශɕ නම් ගාස්තුව රු. 18.15කි. තැපැල් ගාස්තුව රු. 2.50කි. ෙකොළඹ 5, කිරුළපන, මායා මාවත. අංක 132 රජෙය් පකාශන කාර්යාංශෙය් අධිකාරී ෙවත සෑම වර්ෂයකම ෙනොවැම්බර් 30දා ට පථම දායක මුදල් ෙගවා ඉදිරි වර්ෂෙය් දායකත්වය ලබාෙගන විවාද වාර්තා ලබාගත හැකිය. නියමිත දිෙනන් පසුව එවනු ලබන දායක ඉල්ලුම්පත් භාරගනු ෙනොලැෙබ්.

Subscription : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATION BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue, Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late application for subscriptions will not be accepted.
